 Bhikṣuṇā avalokitasiṃhena samudbhāvitaḥ Dharmasamuccayaḥ prathamam udānam jitadharmakāyavargāḥ parivarto hyanityatā  apramādaḥ kāmatṛṣṇe strī ca madyena te daśa     jitavargaḥ maṅgalācaraṇam  om namo dānaṃ śīlaṃ damaḥ kṣāntirmaitrībhūteṣvahiṃsatā  karuṇāmuditopekṣā śāntisamprāptihetavaḥ  Dhs  narakasyāgrahetavaḥ cāpalyaṃ pāpasaṃśleṣaḥ krūratā vitathaṃ vacaḥ  mithyādṛṣṭiḥ pramādaśca udbhavasādhanāni ajñānasevā jaḍa tā ca buddheḥ saddharmanāśaḥ priyamaithunatvam  āhāraśaktiḥ prabalā ca nidrā tiryaggatau ca pravadanti hetum  Dhs  karmaphalam aśubhaṃ trividhaṃ kṛtvā kāyavāṅmanasāṃ dharmaḥ prabhayā vijitaṃ tamaḥ  Dhs  satyādeḥ praśaṃsā mṛṣāvākyaṃ satyahataṃ paiśunyaṃ ca samādhinā  pārūṣyaṃ mārdava jitaṃ abaddhaṃ bandhanā jitam  Dhs  prāṇātipāto maitryā ca steyaṃ dānaiḥ sadā Dhs  bhūtena nirjito bhūto vahninā tarusampadaḥ  pipāsā vijitā toyairjighitsā bhojanaistathā  Dhs  vīryapraśaṃsā siṃhena vijitāḥ sarve mṛgāḥ sattvādhikāśca ye  santāpena mahecchā ca jitā nityaṃ Dhs  dharmasya pravaratvam yena dharmeṇa manujāstaranti bhavasāgaram  saddharmaprabaraḥ prokto na dharmo laukiko hi saḥ  Dhs  kṣetrāṇīmāni catvāri vidyante yasya dehinaḥ  tasyedaṃ saphalaṃ janma bhavati dharmātmā śrutvā pāpaṃ na kurvate  śrutvā karmaphalaṃ jñātvā nirvāṇamadhigacchati  Dhs  śrutvā vedayate dharma śrutvā buddhaḥ prasīdati  śrutvā dharmaṃ vimokṣāya yatate paṇḍito naraḥ  Dhs caturvidhāṃ pratyayitāṃ dharmāṇāṃ codamavyayau  śrutvā tāṃ jñāyate sarvā pumān śraddhāvibhāvitaḥ  Dhs  skandhāyatanadhātūnāṃ yadetallakṣaṇadvayam  śrutvā tajjñāyate sarva tasmāt dharmaparo bhavet  Dhs  prabalā ye trayo doṣāḥ sarvasaṃsārabandhanāḥ  te praṇaśyantyaśeṣeṇa saddharmaśravaṇena vai  Dhs  pravṛtterlakṣaṇaṃ kṛtsnaṃ nivṛtteścāpyaśeṣataḥ  śrutimāṃstat prajānāti tasmācchrutamanuttamam  Dhs Dhs  saddharmanāśaphalam saddharmadhananaṣṭasya guruṇā varjitasya ca  viphalaṃ jīvitaṃ ceṣṭaṃ pāpairupahatasya ca  Dhs  pramādādīnāmaniṣṭaphalasādhanatvam pramādinaḥ kusīdastha pāpamitrasya dehinaḥ narakāgnayaḥ kṛtvā duṣkṛtakarmāṇi sattvā viṣamajīvinaḥ  yā gatiḥ pretya gacchantī tānapāyān hi me śṛṇu  Dhs  sañjīvaṃ kāmasūtraṃ ca sampātaṃ dvau ca rauravau  tamoparaṃ mahācitrapatanaṃ ca pratāpanam  Dhs  ityete narakā aṣṭāvākhyātā duratikramāḥ  raudrakarmābhisaṅkīrṇāḥ pratyekaṃ kṣobhadā matāḥ  Dhs  narakāgnīnāṃ bhayānakatvam catuḥskandhāścaturdvārā vibhaktā bhāgaśo mitāḥ  ayaḥ prākāraparyantā  Dhs  narake patitā bhṛśaṃ tapyante ete patanti narake ūrdhvapādā avāṅmukhāḥ  ṛṣīṇāmativaktāraḥ saṃyatānāṃ tapasvinām  Dhs  te punastatra pacyante taptāmbhasi kṛtā iva  krandamānā divārātrau nagā vāteritā iva  Dhs  praṇadanti mahānādaṃ tīvraduḥkhaiḥ pratāpitāḥ  sarvā diśaśca dhāvanti nārakaiḥ puruṣairdrutāḥ  Dhs  kudṛṣṭyā mohayitvārthe mohapāśāvṛto janaḥ  prāpnoti narakaṃ ghoraṃ parivañcitāḥ  Dhs  kukṛtaphalam yastvayā duṣkṛtaṃ pūrva kṛtaṃ cittānuvartinā  tasya bhuṅktaphalaṃ mūḍha vipākottama māpsyasi  Dhs  hāryāṇi paricittāni saṃsevyāḥ parayoṣitaḥ  hrasvā hi jantavo nityaṃ svacittaparivañcitāḥ  Dhs  tasya karmavipākasya vaśa eva tvamāgataḥ  kiṃ krandasi svayaṃ kṛtvā kukarma puruṣādhama  Dhs  ye narāḥ kukṛtaṃ kṛtvā pañcatvaṃ yāntyamedhasaḥ  yeṣāṃ tu niṣphalaṃ janma bījamuptaṃ yathoṣare  Dhs  alpamādhuryasaṃyuktān kāmān kaṭuvipākinaḥ  sevate yastvasau mūḍhaḥ sa yāti tamaso tamaḥ  Dhs  kiṃ kṛtaṃ mūḍha bhavatā putradārasukhārthinā  dahasye narake caikaḥ svakarmaphalavañcitaḥ  Dhs  keṣāṃ duṣkaraṃ jīvanam yaḥ putradāravaśagaḥ sevate duṣkaraṃ naraḥ  sa yāti narakatvaṃ ca pāpaṃ tadanubhūyate  Dhs  na dārā na sutā nārtha na mitrāṇi kathañcana  mṛtyukāle  Dhs  antargatena ca punarbahiḥsthena ca vahninā  dahyamānohi duḥkhena narake pāpakarmaṇā  Dhs  vaśaṃ prāptāḥ svacittasya sarva eva viḍambitāḥ  kiṃ krandasi vṛthā nāde vahninā paritāpitaḥ  Dhs  Dhs  kasmānna sevito dharmaḥ pāpañca nahi varjitam  pāpād bahiśca puruṣo narakaṃ naiva paśyati  Dhs  yo na vindanti mūḍhātmā phalaṃ pāpasya karttṛkam  so vaśyaṃ labhate doṣān kathaṃ bhokṣyasi durmate  Dhs  pāpena vañcita pūrvaṃ pāpena paridahyate  na kariṣyasi pāpāni tvaduḥkhenaiva yāsyasi  Dhs  kṛtavānasi pāpāni śubhāni na kathañcana  pāpena dahyate tasmādaśubhe na manaḥ kṛthāḥ  Dhs  kiṃ duḥkhādapi duḥkham nāsti duḥkhādato duḥkhaṃ yaḥ pāpamanusevate  tasmāt pāpaṃ na seveta yadi duḥkhaṃ na vāñchasi  Dhs  kuṭumbijanānāṃ spaṣṭoktiḥ tasyāntarhṛdaye bimbaṃ kintu śāntirna vidyate  kāruṇyāspadabhūtāḥ smo nāsmākaṃ karuṇāhṛdi  Dhs  yathā kṛtaṃ bhavadbhiśca pāpaṃ mohāvṛtairbahu  tad vaḥ pradhāvate gāḍhaṃ na ca ye tatra hetavaḥ  Dhs  śīlaṃ na rakṣitaṃ mūḍha pāpaṃ ca bahu sañcitam  sambhūtasya ca pāpasya phalametadupasthitam  Dhs  na vayaṃ kāraṇaṃ tatra yūyameva hi kāraṇam  yaḥ pāpaṃ kurute karma sa hetustasya karmaṇaḥ  Dhs  bhavadbhiryat kṛtaṃ pāpaṃ tṛṣṇāśāpaviḍambitaiḥ  tad vo jvalanopamān  viśuddhadoṣo maṇivacchuddho bhikṣurihocyate  Dhs  antarbahirviśuddhātmā jñānādibhiralaṅkṛtaḥ  śraddhayā śīlavastreṇa kriyāvān bhikṣurucyate  Dhs  lobhadharmavyatīto yaḥ sthito merurivācalaḥ  sarvalokapriyaḥ śāntaḥ pārago bhikṣurucyate  Dhs  trirātrivāsī kutrāpi kuśāsanavidhārakaḥ  girigahvarasevī ca vimukto bhikṣurucyate  Dhs  pāpabhīrurasaṃsparśī saṃvṛtaḥ ca susaṃvṛtaḥ bhikṣoścāraṇyavāsinaḥ  kukaṣāyoktisevāsau mṛtyutaskarajīvikā  Dhs  na hi rājasevako bhikṣuryaḥ sevyo devatairapi  na hiṃsāsavasaṃsṛṣṭo mahate śucisevakaḥ  Dhs  bhikṣoḥ rājasevā na śobhate nirmalasya nirāmasya nispṛhasya ca dehinaḥ  saṃsārabhayabhītasya rājasevā na śobhate  Dhs  vanāraṇyaśmaśāneṣu palvalo giribhūmiṣu  prāntabhūmiṣu grāmasya sthitaḥ bhikṣuḥ praśobhate  Dhs  vanāraṇyaśmaśāneṣu bhikṣurna rājasevayā  dhyānādhyayananirmuktaḥ kavalāhārabhojitā  na bhikṣuriti vijñeyaḥ piśācasamamānasaḥ  Dhs  dhyānāddhi vimalaṃ saukhyaṃ pravadanti manīṣiṇaḥ  na tatsukhātsukhaṃ cānyadasti loke kathañcana  Dhs  taduttamadhyānasukhaṃ muktvā yaḥ puruṣādhamaḥ  raseṣu ramate bālastena mūḍho vihanyate  Dhs  viṣayairbhrāmitasyāsya nityaṃ tadgatacetasaḥ  vardhante kuśalā dharmāḥ paralokāpakarṣakāḥ  Dhs  ātmajño bhikṣurnirvāṇamadhigacchati ātmano yānahīnaśca gurupṛcchanakastathā  bhikṣurudyuktavīryaśca nirvāṇamadhigacchati  Dhs  śrutaṃ yāvad bhavatyeva tāvadeva prabhāṣate  ātmajño mānahīnaśca lābhasatkārayātasya kutaḥ śāntirbhaviṣyati  Dhs  prasannācārayuktasya jñānagocarasevinaḥ  saṃsāradoṣabhītasya pravrajyā saphalā matā  Dhs  svabhāvaparabhāveṣu yasya buddhirnamuñcati  na karmaṇyavipāke  śrāmaṇyadharmasya mahattvam anabhipretamanaso nirāśasya ca dehinaḥ  sarvasaṅgavimuktasya śrāmaṇyaṃ saphalaṃ matam  Dhs  girigahvaravṛkṣeṣu nityaṃ dhyānavihāriṇaḥ  prasīdati śubhaṃ jñānaṃ dharmajño durgati na labhate asaṃśaktā matiryasya mithyākarmasu sarvadā  apakṣapātī dharmajño na sa gacchati durgatim  Dhs  kaḥ munirucyate doṣapaṅkemano yasya na limpati kathañcana  ekārāmavihārīyo  śubhāśubhānāṃ sarveṣāṃ karmaṇāṃ phalatattvavit  śubhāśubhaparityāgī loke sau munirucyate  Dhs  udyukto doṣanāśāya nityakāmagatiḥ smṛtaḥ  udayavyayatattvajño buddhimān munirucyate  Dhs  deśakālavidāṃ Dhs  vīryavān satyavāk bhikṣurnityaṃ doṣavivarjitaḥ  udyānamiva krīḍāyā nirvāṇamadhigacchati  Dhs  kalyāṇadharmī bhava dagdhe kleśe vayaṃ dagdhā vanaṃ dagdhaṃ yathāgninā  kalyāṇadharme saṃraktā na daśa   iti tṛtīyam udānam  atha caturtham udānam puṇyadevasukhairmitrarājastutibhiranvitāḥ  saddharmasmṛtivaipulyai gṛhīto yaṃ samuccayaḥ     puṇyavargaḥ puṇyapraśaṃsā ramaṇīyāni puṇyāni phalaṃ teṣāṃ jyotirjyotiḥparāyaṇaḥ  Dhs  jyotihirjyotiṣā pūrṇa dīpo dīpāntarād yathā  tasmāddhi paramāṃllokān prayātā samprapadyate  Dhs  ācāravān devānāmantikaṃ vrajet yasya śuddhaṃ sadā cittaṃ nirmalaṃ maṇivat sadā  sa śānto nirmamo dhīmān devānāmantikaṃ vrajet  Dhs  dhyānaśīlasamādhibhyo yasya cittaṃ śubhānvitam  sa dhīmān kāñcanaprakhyo devānāmantikaṃ vrajet  Dhs  prāṇātipātād virataḥ sarvasattvadayāparaḥ  ṛtusroto nukampāśca devānāmantikaṃ vrajet  Dhs  śrutavān sarvalokasya krūrakarmavivarjitaḥ  aliptaḥ pāpakairdharmairdevānāmantikaṃ vrajet  Dhs  tṛṇavat kāñcanaṃ yasya kāmā yasya viṣopamāḥ  sa kāmavarjako dhīmān devānāmantikaṃ vrajet  Dhs  nākṛṣyate manaḥ kāmairviṣayai rāgahetubhiḥ  samantātbhavakāntārairdevānāmantikaṃ vrajet  Dhs  bhinnāḥ paramparā ādau mitravān dhanabāndhavaḥ  yaḥ karoti susaṃśliṣṭā devānāmantikaṃ vrajet  Dhs  yasya buddhisthitaṃ veśma na buddhiḥ kvāpi rāgiṇī  sa jitārirviśuddhātmā devānāmantikaṃ vrajet  Dhs  praśastakāyakarmānto yaḥ pāpavirataḥ sukhī  sa kāmavirato dhyāyī devānāmantikaṃ vrajet  Dhs  pāpamitravinirmuktastṛṣṇāviṣavivarjitaḥ  na baddhaḥ strībhayaiḥ pāśairdevānāmantikaṃ vrajet  Dhs  prayatnavādī yo dharme dānaśīlasamādhimān  nityodyukto dṛḍhamatirdevānāmantikaṃ vrajet  Dhs  samyagbandhano yena pāśaśchinno yathāsinā  sacchinnapāśaḥ svavaśī devānāmantikaṃ vrajet  Dhs  śubhakarmavipākena devaloke udbhavaḥ manuṣyabhūtā ye sattvāścaranti sukṛtāvahāḥ  tena karmavipākena suraloke prasūyate  Dhs  dharmapathāśritā eva balinaḥ manuṣyāṇāṃ balād devā devānāṃ balino narāḥ  anyonyabalino te ye saddharmapathamāsthitāḥ  Dhs  tistro pāyabhūmayaḥ devānāṃ sugatirmartyāḥ martyānāṃ sugatiḥ surāḥ  apāyabhūmayastisraḥ śubhakarmavivarjitāḥ  Dhs  sarva sukhaṃ dharmādhīnam dharmādhīnaṃ sukhaṃ sarva dharmādhīnā hi nirvṛtiḥ  dharmaḥ supteṣu jāgarti dharmo hi paramā gatiḥ  Dhs  devairasurā jitāḥ dharmeṇa nirjito dharmaḥ satyenānṛtiko jitaḥ  jñānena varjito moho devaistu hyasurā jitāḥ  Dhs  devalokaṃ sukhodayam sopānabhūtā ye tāni karmāṇi tridivasya hi  yoniṃ tyaktvā narā yānti devalokaṃ sukhodayam  Dhs  vāksaṃyamena budhāstridivaṃ sukhaṃ bhuñjanti caturvidho vāṅniyamaḥ ko pi trividhapañcadhā  saptasopānamārūpyaṃ gacchanti tridivaṃ budhāḥ  Dhs  prabhayā te ca divyantaḥ svaśarīreṇa jātayā  ramante svargabhuvane rañjitāḥ svena karmaṇā  Dhs  śīlameva śubhasya kāraṇam nityāmodavihārāye nityaṃ saukhyavihāriṇaḥ  yad devā devabhavane śīlaṃ tatra hi kāraṇam  Dhs  yadapsaraḥ parivṛtā yat sūryaśaśisannibhāḥ  devāḥ samantād deveṣu tatsarvaśubhahetukam  Dhs  yadīpsitaṃ sambhavati sambhūtaṃ ca na hīyate  vartate ca śubhaṃ nityaṃ tat sarva śubhahetukam  Dhs  śubhacārī devānāṃ samatāṃ vrajet śubhacārī sadā dānī sarvabhūtadayārataḥ  dānamaitryā sadā yukto devānāṃ samatāṃ vrajet  Dhs  prāṇātipātād virataḥ sarvasattvadayāparaḥ  samyagājīvakarmānto devānāṃ saṅgatiṃ vrajet  Dhs  adatte na ratiḥ kiñcid dāne cāsya sadāmatiḥ  śāntendriyamatirdhīmān devasaṅgatimaśnute  Dhs  mithyākāmairvimukto yaḥ satpathābhirataḥ sadā  nirvāṇakāṃkṣī vimalo devānāmantikaṃ vrajet  Dhs  vimanaskaṃ hi yat prīte puruṣe kurute laghu  madyavarjī paraṃ dhīro devānāmantikaṃ vrajet  Dhs  pramādavirahitaḥ sukhamāpnoti sukha prāṇo hi yo devaḥ pramādaṃ nānusevate  sukhāt sukhamavāpnoti nirvṛttiṃ cādhigacchati  Dhs  kṣayāvasānaṃ tat saukhyaṃ nirvāṇamiti śāśvatam  tat saprāpyavimāneṣu rājante puruṣottamāḥ  Dhs  uccāduccaro merustasmāduccaṃ sadā sukham  śubhena niyato janturakaniṣṭhān surān jayet  Dhs  niravadye kutastṛptirdevaloke viśeṣataḥ  atīva saukhyaṃ labhate kasmād deveṣu sarvadā  Dhs  kaḥ saukhyamupalabhyate tṛṣṇāgniparidagdhena na saukhyamupalabhyate  evaṃ sukṛtadagdhena na saukhyamupalabhyate  Dhs  trividhaṃ sukṛtaṃ kṛtvā triprakāraṃ trihetukam  etadagryaṃ tribhūmiṣṭhaṃ triguṇaṃ ca phalaṃ mahat  Dhs  ahiṃsādānaparamā ye saddharmaparāyaṇāḥ  satyakṣāntidamairyuktāḥ tridivaṃte samāgatāḥ  Dhs  divyābharaṇasampannā divyamālyavibhūṣitāḥ  yad devā divyamatayaḥ kurvanti śubhameva tat  Dhs  devānāṃ yanmahatsaukhyaṃna nyūnādhikyamāsthitam  nyūnamadhyaṃ tu yasyaitat phalaṃ puṇyasya dṛśyate  Dhs  puṇyakartā devalokaṃ gacchati yena yāvaddhi yat puṇyaṃ kṛtaṃ bhavati dehinā  tasya tāvaddhi tat saukhyaṃ devalokeṣu pacyate  Dhs  śīlasaṃrakṣaṇamāvaśyakam svāgataṃ tava bho bhadra sukṛtaṃ kṛtavānasi  saptadhā rakṣitaṃ śīlaṃ tasyaitat phalamāgatam  Dhs  ramasva saha daivataiḥ vanopavanaśaileṣu padmākaravaneṣu ca  harmyāgreṣu ramasva tvaṃ kāñcaneṣu sadaivataḥ  Dhs  vanopavanaśaileṣu vaidūryaśikhareṣu ca  vanādriṣu ca naikeṣu ramasva saha daivataiḥ  Dhs  kalpavṛkṣeṣu ramyeṣu nadīprastravaṇeṣu ca  saritsu ca viśālāsu ramasva saha daivataiḥ  Dhs  strotasvinyādiyukteṣu parvateṣu nadīṣu ca  nagareṣu mahārtheṣu ramasva saha daivataiḥ  Dhs  madagandhipraroheṣu nīlotpalavaneṣu ca  yakṣasadmasu ramyeṣu ramasva saha daivataiḥ  Dhs  bhūmibhāgeṣu cānteṣu ratnākaravaneṣu ca  vimāneṣu ca ramyeṣu ramasva saha daivataiḥ  Dhs  pañcāṅgikena tūryeṇa manaḥprahlādakāriṇā  nṛtyamānaḥ sukhī nityaṃ ramasva saha daivataiḥ  Dhs  śīlabījaṃ śodhayitvā śīleṣu vividheṣu ca  krīḍa tvaṃ vividhairdivyairyathārthamanusevase  Dhs  yatprabhāmālino devā ramante vividhaiḥ sukhaiḥ  tacchubhasya phalaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ nirmalasya viśeṣataḥ  Dhs  yadetairvividhaiḥ saukhyairdevāḥ krīḍantyanekaśaḥ  na vayaṃ hetavastatra tatra hetuḥ purākṛtam  Dhs  kūṭāgārāṇi sarvāṇi karmacitrāṇi sarvadā  bhunakti devo deveṣu satkṛtenopabṛṃhitaḥ  Dhs  pāśatrayavimuktasya pañcabhiḥ pālitasya vai  ekadharmavyatītasya devaloko mahīyate  Dhs  pramudyaccetasāṃ puṃsāṃ spaṣṭaceṣṭā samāhitā  āgatā devasadanaṃ svakarmaphalasākṣiṇī  Dhs  sukṛtaphalam uparyupari saukhyāni tathā ca sukṛtasya vai  bhuñjanti vibudhāḥ svarga yaddhi pūrvakṛtānugam  Dhs  sākṣibhūtā ime sarvakarmaṇāṃ vividhā drumāḥ  nirantaraṃ susadṛśaṃ kathayanti manīṣiṇaḥ  Dhs  bhāgyaṃ phalati sarvatra yena yena vipākena yatra yatropapadyate  puruṣo labhate svasya prārabdhasya śubhāśubham  Dhs  śubhakarmaṇā prāṇī nityaṃ deveṣu jāyate śubhena karmaṇā janturnityaṃ deveṣu jāyate  tathāśubhena narake patanti puruṣādhamāḥ  Dhs  kāmino maraṇaṃ nāvagacchanti śubhāśubhābhyāṃ saṃraktāḥ kāminaḥ kāmamohitāḥ  nāvagacchanti maraṇaṃ yadavaśyaṃ bhaviṣyati  Dhs  śubhāśubhavipāko yaṃ yo vṛkṣeṣūpalabhyate  na saukhyād viramantyete manaḥ saukhyena mohitāḥ  Dhs  sukṛtaṃ kṛtvā mānavāḥ deveṣu yānti trividhaṃ sukṛtaṃ kṛtvā bhāvayitvā ca saptadhā  trisaṃkhyākān ripūn hatvā yānti deveṣu mānavāḥ  Dhs  kaḥ devānāmantikaṃ vrajet nāsūyati kriyākleśān na ca nandīmasūyati  sa nandyasūyakaḥ śuddho devānāmantikaṃ gataḥ  Dhs  vinindya mātsaryamidaṃ duḥkhasyāyatanaṃ mahat  samaṃ ca trividhaṃ dattvā devānāmantikaṃ gataḥ  Dhs  prāṇināṃ praṇayaṃ nityaṃ rakṣayitvānukampayā  maitracittaḥ sadā dānto devānāmantikaṃ gataḥ  Dhs  adattaṃ ca dhanaṃ dattvā dattvānandaṃ ca sarvataḥ  cetanābhāvitamatirdevānāmantikaṃ vrajet  Dhs  mātṛvat paradārāṃśca dṛṣṭvā tattvārthacintakaḥ  alipto pāpakairdharmairdevānāmantikaṃ vrajet  Dhs  kṛtaḥ svacittaprītyartha jihvāraṇisamudbhavaḥ  kathyate sa mṛṣāvādastaṃ hitvā sugatiṃ vrajet  Dhs  paiśūnyaṃ ca sadā hitvā maitryanarthakaraṃ padam  ślakṣṇaprabhaḥ ślakṣṇamatiḥ devānāmantikaṃ vrajet  Dhs  pāruṣyaṃ śatruvaddhīro varjayatyeva sarvadā  ślakṣṇaprabhāmatirnityaṃ sarveṣu gatigāmikaḥ  Dhs  adharmo yasya jihvāgre na bhūto na bhaviṣyati  sadā duṣkālatattvajño devānāmantikaṃ vrajet  Dhs  yenedaṃ rakṣitaṃ śīlaṃ saptadhā buddhadeśitam  sa dhīraḥ śīlatattvajño devānāmantikaṃ vrajet  Dhs  kaḥ saphalaḥ dharmajñaḥ vividhakarmavaśagaṃ janmedaṃ labhate suraiḥ  tatprāpya yo na dharmajñaḥ sa paścāt paritapyate  Dhs  sukarmaṇā śubhajaṃ phalam vanopavanaramyo yaṃ latāvedikamaṇḍapaḥ  yadvicitramayo lokastat sarva śubhajaṃ phalam  Dhs  yena yena yathā karma kṛtaṃ bhavati śobhanam  tasya tasya tathā dṛṣṭaṃ phalaṃ tadanugāmikam  Dhs  pratyakṣaṃ dṛśyate devairhīnamadhyottamaṃ sukham  yena yena yathā cīrṇaṃ tasya tasya tathā phalam  Dhs  kukarmaṇā duḥkhajaṃ phalam vicitraveṣāḥ saṃmūḍhā devā mohavaśānugāḥ  tannāśānmanasā mūḍhā na paśyanti mahadbhayam  Dhs  vicitrakāmaratayo vicitraphalakāṅkṣiṇaḥ  na vā kurvanti karmāṇi te surā mūḍhacetasaḥ  Dhs  ke premaparāyaṇāḥ phalaṃ yeṣāṃ priyaṃ cittaṃ na ca śīle ratā matiḥ  te pradīpaṃ parityajya premālokaparāyaṇāḥ  Dhs  hetuphalatattvajñāḥ sukhino bhavanti ye hetuphalasādṛśyenecchanti surasattamān  te hetuphalatattvajñā bhavanti sukhabhāginaḥ  Dhs  jñānādeva muktiḥ vinābījaṃ phalaṃ nāsti vinā dīpaṃ kutaḥ prabhā  vinā śīlaiḥ kutaḥ svargo muktirjñānaṃ vinā kutaḥ  Dhs  kaḥ dhīmataḥ tatsukhaṃ tadvimuktasya gatakāṅkṣasya tāyinaḥ  vimuktakāmatṛṣṇasya nirmamasya ca dhīmataḥ  Dhs  sukarmaiḥ sukhaṃ sadāloko devatāgaṇasevitaḥ  Dhs  virājate girivaro ratnamāṇikyasannibhaḥ  prabhūtasalilo yaśca padminībhiḥ samāvṛtaḥ  Dhs  vanopavanaramyo yaṃ mṛgapakṣiniṣevitaḥ  kandarodarasaṃrambho bhitvā bhavanti sadā dāntāste janāḥsvargagāminaḥ  Dhs  saṃkṣiptamanasaḥ śāntāste janāḥ svargagāminaḥ  vairiṇāṃ viṣayo nityaṃ praśāntamanasastu ye  Dhs  vītarāgā vītamohāste janāḥ svargagāminaḥ  bhavābhavena tīvreṇa bādhate yatra sādhanam  sudāntamānasāṃ dhīrāste janāḥ svargagāminaḥ  Dhs  satyamārgavilambena hayatīva sukhabhāginaḥ  sārāsāravidhijñāśca te janāḥ svargagāminaḥ  Dhs  saṃsāre ye na rakṣanti svamano nanu dehinaḥ  nirvāṇābhiratā nityaṃ te janāḥ svargagāminaḥ  Dhs  vṛkṣamūle śmaśāne vā tathā ca girikandare  dhyāyinaḥ sattvamanasaste janāḥ svargagāminaḥ  Dhs  mātrajñā deśakālajñāḥ pāpamitravivarjitāḥ  maitreṇa cetasā ye tu te janāḥ svargagāminaḥ  Dhs  na snānadarśanaratā narāḥ manmathavāriṇā  ekāntagāminaḥ śāntāste janāḥ svargagāminaḥ  Dhs  kṣaṇe kṣaṇe sadā kāyaṃ madhyatattvāntamanekavidhasambhavam  paśyanti ca na rakṣanti te janāḥ svargagāminaḥ  Dhs  māyopamaṃ ca kṣaṇikaṃ gandharvanagaropamam  ye jānanti sadā cittāḥ te janāḥ svargagāminaḥ  Dhs yeṣāṃ kausīdyadyutiriṣyate  nityodyuktavihārā ye te janāḥ svargagāminaḥ  Dhs  kaukṛtyaṃ styānamiddhaṃ ca kausīdyaṃ ca viśeṣataḥ  varjayanti sadā dhanyāste janāḥ svargagāminaḥ  Dhs  dauḥśīlyaṃ pañcarandhrebhyaḥ pariśuddhamanekadhā  saṃkṣipanti sadā duḥkhaṃ te janāḥ svargagāminaḥ  Dhs  upādānacatuṣṭvajñāḥ satyāni ca tathaiva ca  ye paśyanti budhāḥ prajñāṃ te janāḥ svargagāminaḥ  Dhs  duḥkhaṃ duḥkhavipākaśca duḥkheṣu ca manaśca yat  paśyanti ye sadā tattvaṃ te janāḥ svargagāminaḥ  Dhs  tīvravyasanamāpannā ye ca dharmāvimuñcakāḥ  śāntāśca dharmamatayaste janāḥ svargagāminaḥ  Dhs  śuklāvadātaṃ ye vastraṃ pāṃsukūlaṃ tathaiva ca  piṇḍapātaratā nityaṃ te janāḥ svargagāminaḥ  Dhs  adaṇḍāḥ śāntamanaso nityaṃ dhyānavihāriṇaḥ  naiṣkarmyaniratāḥ sarve te janāḥ svargagāminaḥ  Dhs  mṛṣṭaṃ ca yadi vāṅmṛṣṭaṃ yathecchāvidhimāgatam  santuṣyanti na kupyanti te janāḥ svargagāminaḥ  Dhs  śuklāvadātaṃ ye vastraṃ pāṃsukūlaṃ tathaiva ca  saṃvṛtau caiva saṃtuṣṭāste janāḥ svargagāminaḥ  Dhs  śayyātale yathā bhūmau harmyāgre vā tathāpare  na duṣyanti na hṛṣyanti te janāḥ svargagāminaḥ  Dhs  cakṣurviṣayamāpannaṃ yatkarma sāmparāyikam  tattvato ye prapaśyanti te janāḥ svargagāminaḥ  Dhs yathā karma kṛtaṃ sarvamaviśeṣeṇa tattvataḥ  paśyantyamanaso dhanyāste janāḥ svargagāminaḥ  Dhs  karmaṇāṃ ca vipākaṃ ca kṛtaṃ ye dhīracetasā  bibhyatīha sadā duḥkhete janāḥ svargagāminaḥ  Dhs  ityetāni mahārthāni nityaṃ duḥkhakarāṇi ca  kurvanti vidhivat sarva te janāḥ svargagāminaḥ  Dhs   iti devavargo dvātriṃśaḥ   sukhavargaḥ sukhasvarūpanirūpaṇam anuttareṣu saukhyeṣu dhyānopātteṣu ye ratāḥ  teṣāṃ sukhaṃ yathāvat syāt nirvāṇapuradarśakam  Dhs  navena sukhaduḥkhena purāṇamabhihanyate  devasyaitannavenaiva purāṇamabhihanyate  Dhs  dhūma miśraṃ yathā kāṣṭhaṃ viṣṭhā miśraṃ yathodanam  tathā sukhamidaṃ sarvamasvatvaṃ nāvagamyate  Dhs  nirvāṇapuragāmināṃ sukham tat sukhaṃ yad vitṛṣṇānāmekāntasukhacāriṇām  nirmohiṇāmarāgāṇāṃ nirvāṇapuragāminām  Dhs  teṣāṃ vimalamādyantaṃ saukhyānāmapi tat sukham  yeṣāṃ tṛṣṇānugā cāśā sarvathā naiva cetasi  Dhs  saṅgṛhītasya cittasya nirātmasya ca sarvataḥ  kāryākāryeṣu mūḍhasya sukhaṃ nityamupasthitam  Dhs  kaḥ śreṣṭhaḥ sukhī sā bahirnihatā yena nandisaṃsārahetukī  sa dhīraḥ pāragaḥ śreṣṭhaḥ sukhī nirvāṇamāśritaḥ  Dhs  naitat sukhena tṛṣṇānāṃ yad rāgadveṣasaṃyutam  yatra rāgādinirmuktaṃ tat sukhaṃ nirmalaṃ matam  Dhs  kutra tṛṣṇā na bādhate devaloke samāsādya yaḥ suro nāvamanyate  sa sukhāt sukhatāṃ yāti yatra tṛṣṇā na bādhate  Dhs  tadantyasukhi śreyo yatra mṛtyurna vidyate  mṛtyupāśairna baddhasya na sukhaṃ vidyate kvacit  yat sukhaṃ kāmajanakaṃ na tat saukhyaṃ satāṃ matam  Dhs  yatra kāmavinirmuktastatsukhāt sukhamuttamam  yat sukhaṃ janayet śreyaḥ payomiśraṃ yathodanam  Dhs  yatra tṛṣṇāvinirmuktiḥ payomiśraṃ yathodanam  yathā padmavane gṛddhā yāntite kravyabhakṣiṇaḥ  Dhs  evaṃ śānteṣvaraṇyeṣu na bhāntyaśubhacāriṇaḥ  kvacicchāntaṃ vanaṃ ramyaṃ kvacid devāḥ pramādinaḥ  Dhs  kaḥ paramaṃ sukhaṃ prāpnoti viparītaṃ na sadṛśaṃ bhānoḥ śītā yathā prabhā  gatatṛṣṇasya yat saukhyaṃ muktaduḥkhasya tāyinaḥ  Dhs  tasyāntareṇa saukhyasya sukhametanna gaṇyate  dhyāyinastvapramattasya muktapāpasya sarvadā  Dhs  tat sukhaṃ tat paraṃ saukhyaṃ nedaṃ tṛṣṇāvidāṃ matam  munisevyaṃ vanamidaṃ sevitaṃ ca subhāṣitaiḥ  Dhs  nārhā yūyaṃ rāgagaṇaṃ sevituṃ bho surottamāḥ  yadetad bhavatāṃ saukhyametanna khalu śāśvatam  Dhs  tat sukhaṃ paramaṃ śāntaṃ vītatṛṣṇai niṣevyate  niḥsevitaṃ vanamidaṃ ye gatāḥ paramaṃ padam  Dhs  yat prāpya sarvaduḥkhasyacchedo bhavati sarvathā  brahmacaryādanirmuṣṭāḥ śīlālāpena vañcitāḥ  Dhs  bhikṣūṇāṃ vane vāsa eva sukhāvahaḥ nārhanti sevituṃ ramyaṃ vanaṃ śāntaṃ subhāṣitam  śāntaṃ ca bhāvitaṃ caiva ramate śubhagocare  Dhs  na rāgacāriṇāṃ cittaṃ ramate vanagocare  na rāgavyākulaṃ cittaṃ vaneṣu labhate dhṛtim  Dhs  kaḥ puruṣottamaḥ śravyāmūḍhā matiryasya nityaṃ tribhuvanaṃ kare  sa ratiṃ labhate śāntiṃ vane puruṣasattamaḥ  Dhs  sukhāya vanaṃ sevyam sa kalparāgakuṭilo nityaṃ rāgādibhirvṛtaḥ  sa śāntiṃ naiva labhate vane śānte sukhāvahe  Dhs  yeṣāṃ tu manasā nityaṃ vane dhyānaniyoginām  vanaṃ teṣāṃ sadāramyaṃ na tu rāgagaveṣiṇām  Dhs  vaneṣu bhāvitaṃ cittaṃ nagareṣu na kupyate  tasmād vanaṃ sadā sevyaṃ nagaraṃ naiva śasyate  Dhs  vikṣipyate hi nagare nṛṇāṃ rāgādibhirvṛtaḥ  vikṣipta mohakuṭilaṃ vanaṃ bhūyaḥ prasīdati  Dhs  tasmād vanaṃ paraṃ śāntaṃ yogināmālayaṃ mahat  saṃsevyaṃ vītamanasā yasya tad vītakalmaṣam  Dhs  ratiṃ mā kṛthā praśāntendriyacittasya yā ratiryogino hṛdi  nāsau śaktiḥ sahasrasya mānavānāṃ bhaviṣyati  Dhs  yā dhyāyino ratirdṛṣṭā vyavadānāya sarvadā  na yāmeṣvapi sā dṛṣṭā nityaṃ rāgānurāgiṇī  Dhs  ratiryā kāmavaśagā sā nityaṃ duḥkhasambhavā  yā tu kleśavaśāt prītiḥ sā prītiḥ śāśvatā nahi  Dhs  kaḥ śreyaspadaṃ prāpnoti śreyo vaneṣu caritaṃ tattaduccaritaṃ nṛbhiḥ  yasmāt tat pratibaddhaṃ hi śreyasāṃ padamucyate  Dhs  susambhṛtena dharmeṇa rakṣiteneva cetasā  sudṛṣṭaṃ labhate sthānaṃ yatra doṣo na vidyate  Dhs  yaḥ kṣiptamanasā nityaṃ na ca dharmaparāyaṇaḥ  teṣāṃ vṛthā sukhamidaṃ gacchati na nivartate  Dhs  tattvajñā duḥkhaṃ na paśyanti ye tu tattvavido dhīrāḥ paśyanti jagataḥ sthitim  anityaduḥkhaśūnyānāṃ teṣāṃ duḥkhaṃ na vidyate  Dhs  sukhadharmasya caraṇaṃ udayavyayadharmāṇāmanityaṃ karmajaṃ hi tat  tat sukhaṃ sāstravaṃ nityaṃ na bhūtaṃ na bhaviṣyati  Dhs  tat sukhaṃ tadvitṛṣṇasya nīrāgasya hi dehinaḥ  muktirbhavati doṣasya pārasthasya hi tāpinaḥ  Dhs nirvāṇasukhagāminaḥ  Dhs  anupāyena ye mūḍhāḥ prārthayanti sukhaṃ sadā  bālukābhiryathā tailaṃ yallabhyaṃ nityameva tat  Dhs  na cetasā naraḥ prājño manorathaśatairapi  śakro pi tat sukhaṃ kartu yathā karma kṛtaṃ mahat  Dhs  sukhāya dharmamācaret sasukhaṃ yasya tu manaḥ saddharmānucaro bhavet  duḥkhairmuktyabhilāṣo yaṃ sa dharme kurute matim  Dhs  nāhetukaṃ sukhaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ duḥkhaṃ vā trividhātmakam  sukhe duḥkhe pṛthagbhāve tasmānnu sukṛta caret  Dhs  nedaṃ saukhyaṃ sadā śastamadhruvaṃ vipralopi ca  tṛṣṇāviṣeṇa sammiśraṃ viṣamiśraṃ yathodanam  Dhs  tat saukhyaṃ hi satāṃ śastaṃ yatra mṛtyurna duḥkhajanakaṃ kathaṃ tat sukhamiṣyate duḥkhād duḥkhataraṃ jñeyaṃ pariṇāmavaśena tat  Dhs  yadetad bhujyate saukhyametat kālena naśyati  sūryastāstaṅgatasyaivaṃ raśmayaḥ saha cāriṇaḥ  Dhs  vikṛtiṃ yasya ca manaḥ sukhaduḥkhairna gacchati  sa dhīmān suraloke ca gatvānyallabhate sukham  Dhs  bhuktaṃ sukhaṃ purāṇaṃ tu hīnakarma karoti ca  purāṇaṃ sukṛtaṃ śīrṇa mṛtyukāle na budhyate  Dhs  sarva sukhamanityaṃ bhavati yadidaṃ dṛśyate saukhyaṃ manovākkāmajaṃbhṛśam  anityaṃ tad vināśatvamacireṇa bhaviṣyati  Dhs  phenabudbudasaṅkāśaṃ marīcyudakasannibham  cañcalormi sukhaṃ sarva vinipāto  Dhs  laukikaṃ sukhaṃ na sukham yad sukhaṃ triṣu lokeṣu na śastaṃ tattvadarśibhiḥ  tena matvā kathaṃ devā bhavanti vigatajvarāḥ  Dhs  aviṣṭovatakālo yaṃ bhairavo yāti sattvaram  yo bhokṣyate surān sukhaṃ duḥkhasadṛśaṃ bhavati yadatyantasukhaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ tat sukhaṃ satyamucyate  yatra duḥkhaṃ vipākaṃ syāt tat sukhaṃ duḥkhameva tat  Dhs  pāpasyākaraṇameva sukham anyāgatasya duḥkhasya pratighātayate Dhs  nānādṛṣṭivibhedāya sarvasaṃśayamocine  samyagdṛṣṭiniveśāya namaḥ sañjñānacakṣuṣe  Dhs  sarvasaṅkaṭabhedāya tridoṣamalaśodhine  namo nakṣatrabhūtāya sarvabījaphaloruhe  Dhs  sarvaprajñākarāgrāya śāntamānasaḥ  sa mucyate bhavabhayānnivṛttiṃ cādhigacchati  Dhs  etacchāntapadaṃ ramyametannaiṣṭhikamucyate  yadayaṃ bhāṣate dharma nirvāṇapuradeśikaḥ  Dhs  asya vākyaṃ samālambya puruṣādhīnavikramāḥ  ākarṣanti padaṃ nityaṃ yadanantasukhāvaham  Dhs  etat pūrva samāruhaya puruṣāstattvacintakāḥ  trilokaughārṇavaṃ ghoraṃ taranti bhavasāgaram  Dhs  ayaṃ sa cakṣurlokasya samantāddhi vicakṣuṣaḥ  ayaṃ jyotiḥ paraṃ jyotiryajjyotiḥkāṣṭhasambhavam  Dhs  kalpāntaṃ prāṇināṃ citte nṛṇāṃ rāgādibhirmalaiḥ  jñānatoyena mahatā śodhayatyeva vāṅnṛpaḥ  Dhs  yanna dṛṣṭaṃ padaṃ sarvaistīrthikairjñānapāṇibhiḥ  tatpadaṃ vimalairvākyaistvayā nṛṇāṃ pradarśitam  Dhs  pramādaparamo nātho jano yaṃ tāritastvayā  tīrṇaḥ pāragato nāthastārayatyaghanāśanāt  Dhs  hitārtha sarvajagatastvamevaiko vyavasthitaḥ  ahitānāṃ hitāyaiva tvameva puruṣottamaḥ  Dhs  anādimati saṃsāre nṛṇāṃ kleśāpahārakaiḥ  tvayā viśodhito vākyaistamaḥ sūryodaye yathā  Dhs  akṣayaḥ sarvadharmāṇāṃ jñānalokakaro mahān  tvamevaiko jagannātha lokottaraguṇārṇavaḥ  Dhs   iti stutivargaḥ ṣaṭtriṃśaḥ  puṇyadevasukhairmitrarājastutibhiranvitāḥ  saddharmasmṛtivaipulyai gṛhīto yaṃ samuccayaḥ   iti caturtham udānam  ye ca dharmā hetubhavā teṣāṃ tathāgato vadat  teṣāṃ ca yo nirodhaścaivaṃvādīmahāśramaṇaḥ  puṇyamavāptamantrakleśaṃ vibhidyājanavalāśrīkam  yāvajjagadvyākulaṃ tarkaniṣṭhaiḥ samākulaṃ vetti satyavacanaiḥ  vaipulyamahāgambhīrodadhisūtravarād bhikṣuṇā avalokitasiṃhenoddhṛtamiti  mohāśivādirahitasya vākyavidyasya vipulārjanasya dharmasamuccayo nāma dharmaparyāyaḥ samāptaḥ   iti śubham
